# <a name="class-store-class"></a><span data-ttu-id="821fe-105">Classe Class-Store</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="821fe-105">Class-Store class</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="821fe-106">Essa classe é usada para criar o contêiner da classe Store.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="821fe-106">This class is used to create the class store container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="821fe-107">O contêiner Class Store fornece a estrutura para implantar recursos do aplicativo no Active Directory e disponibilizar a política de implantação para os destinatários da política (ou seja, usuários e computadores).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="821fe-107">The class store container provides the framework for deploying application resources in Active Directory and making the deployment policy available to policy recipients (that is, users and computers).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="821fe-108">Os privilégios de acesso e administração são controlados pelas propriedades de controle de acesso padrão no objeto contêiner de armazenamento de classe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="821fe-108">Access and administration privileges are controlled by standard access control properties on the class store container object.</span></span>
